                     <div class="blogher_content">
                      <h3 style="text-align: center;">
                       An easy life hack to make Thin Mints
                       <strong>
                        
                       </strong>
                       Hot Fudge Sauce usingCoffee-mateGirl Scouts Thin Mints Flavored creamer+ $100 Visa Gift Card Giveaway! For those times whenGirl Scouts cookies aren't available.
                      </h3>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-s8mw1hVcUYI/VRS993kVP6I/AAAAAAAAXsk/t6nIC4PW9H8/s1600/Coffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B(1%2Bof%2B1).jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">

                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a data-pin-color="red" data-pin-config="beside" data-pin-do="buttonPin" href="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.serenabakessimplyfromscratch.com%2F2014%2F08%2Fcoffee-mate-girl-scouts-thin-mints_26.html&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-mGFykUSsN_s%2FU-uyE53vINI%2FAAAAAAAAU2I%2FFKKgnrBf-l8%2Fw858-h1296-no%2FCoffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B(1%2Bof%2B1).jpg&amp;description=Coffee-mate%C2%AE%20Girl%20Scouts%C2%AE%20Thin%20Mints%C2%AE%20Flavored%20Hot%20Fudge%20Sauce%20%23LifeHack">

                       When I was in
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2FG5PEqQ" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                        <span data-mce-mark="1">

                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <span data-mce-mark="1">
                        <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2FG5PEqQ" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                        </a>
                        we had some wonderful troop leaders who spent a lot of time teaching us to be resourceful and creative.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <span data-mce-mark="1">
                        <span data-mce-mark="1">
                         <span data-mce-mark="1">
                          We made butter from scratch, learned to sew, and replanted trees in an area that needed it; but one of my favorite things was when it was time to sell cookies.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       I loved the fact my Granny would stock up onThin Mints for an after lunch treat or dessert.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       It's one of those cookies you can never tire of.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       So when I was having a craving forThin Mints the other night, I used my smart cookieskills that I
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       learned inGirl Scoutsto make a Life Hack for a quick Hot Fudge Sauce... what's not to love?

                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-UUryPGv6WS8%2FU-uy7Wp2vAI%2FAAAAAAAAU2c%2Fy1V2yEHyQcQ%2Fw858-h1296-no%2FCoffee%252BMate%252BGirl%252BScout%252BThin%252BMint%252BHot%252BFudge%252BHack%252B%282%252Bof%252B1%29.jpg" rel="nofollow">
                        <img alt="Coffee-mate-Girl-Scouts-Thin-Mint-Flavored-Hot-Fudge-Sauce-Morning-Coffee.jpg" border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UUryPGv6WS8/U-uy7Wp2vAI/AAAAAAAAU2c/y1V2yEHyQcQ/w858-h1296-no/Coffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B(2%2Bof%2B1).jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <span data-mce-mark="1">
                        <span data-mce-mark="1">
                         <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fbit.ly%2F1oyPg5W" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                          Coffee-mate
                         </a>
                         Girl Scouts creamer in
                        </span>
                        <span data-mce-mark="1">
                         Thin Mints flavor is the perfect addition to my morning coffee. I can never pass on
                        </span>
                        <span data-mce-mark="1">
                         Girl Scouts cookies and now I can enjoy all the delicious cookie taste, all year long!
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <span data-mce-mark="1">
                        It makes rolling out of bed a whole lot easier.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-Q0VeHhGOdJo%2FU-u0dBZ9I-I%2FAAAAAAAAU3E%2FCFHKUU41B7w%2Fw1916-h1270-no%2FCoffee%252BMate%252BGirl%252BScout%252BThin%252BMint%252BHot%252BFudge%252BHack%252B%284%252Bof%252B1%29.jpg" rel="nofollow">
                        <img alt="Coffee-mate-Girl-Scouts-Thin-Mint-Flavored-Hot-Fudge-Sauce-Creamer-Chocolate-Chips.jpg" border="0" height="422" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q0VeHhGOdJo/U-u0dBZ9I-I/AAAAAAAAU3E/CFHKUU41B7w/w1916-h1270-no/Coffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B(4%2Bof%2B1).jpg" title="" width="640"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       To make Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mints Flavor Hot Fudge Sauce all you need is 1/2 cup Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mints Flavor Creamer and 1 cup Chocolate Chips.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2F3.bp.blogspot.com%2Fe6QgeP-DzwUBiy2eVCkGaxbrkAxFGuEDzcZfeibCZRph%3Dw858-h1296-no" rel="nofollow">
                        <img alt="Coffee-mate-Girl-Scouts-Thin-Mint-Flavored-Hot-Fudge-Sauce.jpg" border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/e6QgeP-DzwUBiy2eVCkGaxbrkAxFGuEDzcZfeibCZRph=w858-h1296-no" title="" width="424"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       Stir over medium heat until chocolate is melted and smooth.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2F4.bp.blogspot.com%2FME4TqcQeBlutAjrOqCDzbcijfGER3N44hFNhLQ4ULuOn%3Dw858-h1296-no" rel="nofollow">
                        <img alt="Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mint Flavored Hot Fudge Sauce over Ice Cream #CMSmartCookie" border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/ME4TqcQeBlutAjrOqCDzbcijfGER3N44hFNhLQ4ULuOn=w858-h1296-no" title="" width="424"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       Serve over the top of your favorite ice cream or drizzle over the top of your morning coffee for an extra special treat.
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-mGFykUSsN_s%2FU-uyE53vINI%2FAAAAAAAAU2I%2FFKKgnrBf-l8%2Fw858-h1296-no%2FCoffee%252BMate%252BGirl%252BScout%252BThin%252BMint%252BHot%252BFudge%252BHack%252B%281%252Bof%252B1%29.jpg" rel="nofollow">
                        <img alt="Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mint Flavored Hot Fudge Sauce #CMSmartCookie" border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mGFykUSsN_s/U-uyE53vINI/AAAAAAAAU2I/FKKgnrBf-l8/w858-h1296-no/Coffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B(1%2Bof%2B1).jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       So good I promise it won't disappoint!
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       To learn more about all the fun experiences girls and volunteers have at Girl Scouts, visit
                       <a href="http://www.blogher.com/clicktracker.php?nid=1681037&amp;cid=1644460&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fgoo.gl%2FG5PEqQ" rel="nofollow">
                        www.girlscouts.org/join
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="text-align: center;">
                       One last thing before the recipe....
                      </div>

                      <div class="hrecipe">
                       <div class="fn">
                       </div>
                       <div class="fn">
                       </div>
                       <div class="fn">
                       </div>
                       <div class="fn">
                        Hot Fudge Sauce
                       </div>
                       <div class="fn">
                        Recipe by Serena Bakes Simply From Scratch
                       </div>
                       <img alt="Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mint Flavored Hot Fudge Sauce #CMSmartCookie" class="photo" height="200" src="https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-mGFykUSsN_s/U-uyE53vINI/AAAAAAAAU2I/FKKgnrBf-l8/w858-h1296-no/Coffee%2BMate%2BGirl%2BScout%2BThin%2BMint%2BHot%2BFudge%2BHack%2B%281%2Bof%2B1%29.jpg" title="" width="132"/>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="summary">
                        Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mints Flavored Hot Fudge Sauce. An easy Life Hack to make Hot Fudge.
                       </div>
                       Prep time:
                       <span class="preptime">
                        PT2M
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       Cook time:
                       <span class="cooktime">
                        PT3M
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       Total time:
                       <span class="duration">
                        PT5M
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       Yield:
                       <span class="yield">
                        5 Servings
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       Ingredients
                       <br/>
                       <ul>
                        <li class="ingredient">
                         <span class="amount">
                          1/2 cup
                         </span>
                         Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mints Flavored Creamer
                        </li>
                        <li class="ingredient">
                         <span class="amount">
                          1 cup
                         </span>
                         <span class="name">
                          Chocolate Chips
                         </span>
                        </li>
                        <li class="ingredient">
                         <span class="name">
                          For Serving: Ice Cream
                         </span>
                        </li>
                       </ul>
                       Cooking Directions
                       <br/>
                       <ol class="instructions">
                        <li class="instruction">
                         In a small saucepan add Coffee-mate Girl Scouts Thin Mints flavored creamer and Chocolate Chips.
                        </li>
                        <li class="instruction">
                         Stir over medium heat until melted and smooth.
                        </li>
                        <li class="instruction">
                         Serve over your favorite ice cream.
                        </li>
                       </ol>
                       <br/>

      var config = {'blogId': '679376249136878227', 'postId': '7868888979175847812', 'feed': 'http://www.serenabakessimplyfromscratch.com/feeds/7868888979175847812/comments/default', 'authorName': 'Serena Bakes Simply From Scratch', 'authorUrl': 'https://www.blogger.com/profile/15497132642509064238', 'baseUri': 'https://www.blogger.com', 'maxThreadDepth': 2};

      var cursor = null;
      if (items &amp;&amp; items.length &gt; 0) {
        cursor = parseInt(items[items.length - 1].timestamp) + 1;
      }

      var bodyFromEntry = function(entry) {
        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '&lt;span class="deleted-comment"&gt;' + entry.content.$t + '&lt;/span&gt;';
            }
          }
        }
        return entry.content.$t;
      }

      var parse = function(data) {
        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];
        if (data &amp;&amp; data.feed &amp;&amp; data.feed.entry) {
          for (var i = 0, entry; entry = data.feed.entry[i]; i++) {
            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author &amp;&amp; entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {
                comment.author = {
                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };
              }
            }
            if (entry.link) {
              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid &amp;&amp; pid[1]) {
                  comment.parentId = pid[1];
                }
              }
            }
            comment.deleteclass = 'item-control blog-admin';
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
              for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
                if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.itemClass') {
                  comment.deleteclass += ' ' + entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                } else if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.displayTime') {
                  comment.displayTime = entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].value;
                }
              }
            }
            comments.push(comment);
          }
        }
        return comments;
      };

      var paginator = function(callback) {
        if (hasMore()) {
          var url = config.feed + '?alt=json&amp;v=2&amp;orderby=published&amp;reverse=false&amp;max-results=50';
          if (cursor) {
            url += '&amp;published-min=' + new Date(cursor).toISOString();
          }
          window.bloggercomments = function(data) {
            var parsed = parse(data);
            cursor = parsed.length &lt; 50 ? null
                : parseInt(parsed[parsed.length - 1].timestamp) + 1
            callback(parsed);
            window.bloggercomments = null;
          }
          url += '&amp;callback=bloggercomments';
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.type = 'text/javascript';
          script.src = url;
          document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
      };
      var hasMore = function() {
        return !!cursor;
      };
      var getMeta = function(key, comment) {
        if ('iswriter' == key) {
          var matches = !!comment.author
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.name == config.authorName
              &amp;&amp; comment.author.profileUrl == config.authorUrl;
          return matches ? 'true' : '';
        } else if ('deletelink' == key) {
          return config.baseUri + '/delete-comment.g?blogID='
               + config.blogId + '&amp;postID=' + comment.id;
        } else if ('deleteclass' == key) {
          return comment.deleteclass;
        }
        return '';
      };

      var replybox = null;
      var replyUrlParts = null;
      var replyParent = undefined;

      var onReply = function(commentId, domId) {
        if (replybox == null) {
          // lazily cache replybox, and adjust to suit this style:
          replybox = document.getElementById('comment-editor');
          if (replybox != null) {
            replybox.height = '250px';
            replybox.style.display = 'block';
            replyUrlParts = replybox.src.split('#');
          }
        }
        if (replybox &amp;&amp; (commentId !== replyParent)) {
          document.getElementById(domId).insertBefore(replybox, null);
          replybox.src = replyUrlParts[0]
              + (commentId ? '&amp;parentID=' + commentId : '')
              + '#' + replyUrlParts[1];
          replyParent = commentId;
        }
      };

      var hash = (window.location.hash || '#').substring(1);
      var startThread, targetComment;
      if (/^comment-form_/.test(hash)) {
        startThread = hash.substring('comment-form_'.length);
      } else if (/^c[0-9]+$/.test(hash)) {
        targetComment = hash.substring(1);
      }

      // Configure commenting API:
      var configJso = {
        'maxDepth': config.maxThreadDepth
      };
      var provider = {
        'id': config.postId,
        'data': items,
        'loadNext': paginator,
        'hasMore': hasMore,
        'getMeta': getMeta,
        'onReply': onReply,
        'rendered': true,
        'initComment': targetComment,
        'initReplyThread': startThread,
        'config': configJso,
        'messages': msgs
      };

      var render = function() {
        if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
          var holder = document.getElementById('comment-holder');
          window.goog.comments.render(holder, provider);
        }
      };

      // render now, or queue to render when library loads:
      if (window.goog &amp;&amp; window.goog.comments) {
        render();
      } else {
        window.goog = window.goog || {};
        window.goog.comments = window.goog.comments || {};
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue = window.goog.comments.loadQueue || [];
        window.goog.comments.loadQueue.push(render);
      }

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_6MC">
                             Any stain on a carpet- sprinkle with baking soda and let set 10 minutes or more.  Vacuum the baking soda up and then mix 2-3 drops of Dawn with 2 T. vinegar in a bowl of warm water.  Use cloth to scrub spot using mixture and let dry completely.  If some remains, repeat.  This has worked on some really tough stains on our carpets!
                            </p>

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_17MC">
                             My favorite hack to make extra crispy bacon with less fat is to flip over a microwaveable bowl and put it on a plate. Cover the bowl with paper towels and then lay the bacon over the bowl and top with another paper towel. As the bacon cooks the grease falls into the plate!
                            </p>

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_24MC">
                             I buy large bags of snacks (goldfish, etc) at Costco, then bag them in snack sized Ziploc bags.  Even with the cost of the bags, they are way cheaper than buying the individual serving packages.  Then I put all the healthy snacks together in a drawer, so that the kids can just go pick whatever they want, and I know it will be something healthy.  (BTW: I love your blog so much!)

                            <div class="comment-header" id="bc_0_49M" kind="m">

                             <span class="datetime secondary-text">
                              <a href="http://www.serenabakessimplyfromscratch.com/2014/08/coffee-mate-girl-scouts-thin-mints_26.html?showComment=1409466615346#c4128711578509571080" rel="nofollow">

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_49MC">
                             Wow, I can't wait to try this on some ice cream!!! My life hack...I like to use vinegar solution for cleaning just about anything. I don't need to buy a different cleaner for every job. It works for cleaning pet stains too Fresh stains, never tried it on a set in stain. Just use 1/2 cup vinegar (regular, not apple cider vinegar) to 1/2 gallon warm water. Apply to spot liberally. Rinse with plain water. Repeat as needed until it's gone. The vinegar smell dissipates quickly and it doesn't leave a soapy residue. Plus the dog/cat won't be able to smell where the deed was done and re-spoil the area
                            </p>
                            <span class="comment-actions secondary-text" id="bc_0_49MN" kind="m">
                             <a href="javascript:;" kind="i" o="r" target="_self">

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_55MC">
                             My favorite life hack is laying out all the breakfast items the night before including spoons, etc. It makes mornings so much simpler and makes my children quieter. I also love to slice a lemon and put it in a bowl of water in the microwave to get rid of odors and make for an easy way to clean it.

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_97MC">
                             I give each of our five kids two laundry hampers. Darks/lights. I do laundry for one person at a time. I no longer have to sort loads before washing and I do not have to sort things and ask "Who does this belong to?" when things come out of the dryer. I wish I had started doing this years sooner!

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_131MC">
                             I don't bother cooking bacon on the stovetop at all, it's too messy and doesn't yield evenly cooked bacon sometimes. I put cooling rack inside one of my half sheet pans and lay the bacon on top of the rack. It cooks perfectly with the grease draining away and it stays nice and straight. I also like to line the sheet pan with foil to make for easy cleanup too!
                            </p>

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_134MC">
                             My life hack is using imitation vanilla and water to clean my microwave. Just put a TBSP of vanilla and 1 cup of water in a microwave safe bowl for 1 minute and 30 seconds and proceed to clean. All the food and gunk comes right off plus it smells great!

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_148MC">
                             My life hack is using small bottles that I can keep on top of my washing machine for all of my different cleaners and keeping larger refills on the floor.  That way I have handy access to all I use but don't have to pay for the smaller bottles and can still get the good deals on the bulk sizes!
